isSpeakingRef = useRef(false);\n\n  // Initialize speech recognition singleton\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\n    \n    synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\n    \n    if (!globalRecognition) {\n      const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n      if (SR) {\n        globalRecognition = new SR();\n        globalRecognition.continuous = true;\n        globalRecognition.interimResults = true;\n        globalRecognition.lang = 'en-US';\n      }\n    }\n    \n    if (autoStart) {\n globalRecognition.onstart = () => {\n      globalIsActive = true;\n      setState('listening');\n    };\n\n    globalRecognition.onresult = async (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n      let 'no-speech') return;\n      console.error('[UnifiedBar] Error:', event.error);\n    };\n\n    globalRecognition.onend = () => {\n      globalIsActive = false;\n      if (shouldRunRef.current && !isSpeakingRef.current) {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          if (shouldRunRef.current && !globalIsActive && !isSpeakingRef.current) {\n            safeStart();\n          }\n        }, 500);\n      } else {\n        setState('idle');\n      }\n    };\n  }, [onTranscript, fields, context]);\n\n  const safeStart = () => {\n    if (!globalRecognition || globalIsActive) return;\n    try { globalRecognition.start(); } catch {}\n  };\n\n  // Process voice input - extract data and fill fields\n  const processVoiceInput = async (text: string) => {\n    setState('processing');\n    \n    try {\n      // Send to backend for analysis\n      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/voice/command', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ text, context, user_type: 'user' })\n      });\n      \n      const data = await response.json();\n      \n      // Handle commands\n      onCommand?.(text);\n      \n      // Fill form fields if we got formData\n      if (data?.formData?.fields) {\n        await fillFields(data.formData.fields);\n      }\n      \n      // Speak 'listening' : 'idle');\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Fill fields with typewriter effect\n  const fillFields = async (formData: Record<string, string>) => {\n    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(formData)) {\n      if (!value) continue;\n      \n      const fieldConfig = fields[key];\n      if (!fieldConfig) continue;\n      \n      const element = document.querySelector(fieldConfig.selector) as HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement;\n      if (!element) continue;\n      \n      setFilling(key);\n      element.focus();\n      element.classList.add('vv-filling');\n      \n      // Typewriter effect\n      element.value = '';\n      for (let i = 0; i <= value.length; i++) {\n        element.value = value.substring(0, i);\n        element.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));\n        element.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));\n        \n        // Call setter if provided\n        if (fieldConfig.setter) {\n          fieldConfig.setter(value.substring(0, i));\n        }\n        \n        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 25));\n      }\n      \n      element.classList.remove('vv-filling');\n      element.classList.add('vv-filled');\n      setTimeout(() => element.classList.remove('vv-filled'), 1000);\n      \n      // Final setter call\n      if (fieldConfig.setter) {\n        fieldConfig.setter(value);\n      }\n      \n      setFilling(null);\n      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 200));\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Text-to-speech\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    if (externalSpeak) {\n      externalSpeak(text);\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    if (!synthRef.current) return;\n    \n    const wasRunning = shouldRunRef.current;\n    isSpeakingRef.current = true;\n    \n    // Stop listening while speaking\n    if (globalIsActive && globalRecognition) {\n      try { globalRecognition.stop(); } catch {}\n    }\n    \n    synthRef.current.cancel();\n    setState('speaking');\n    \n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    utterance.rate = 0.95;\n    \n    utterance.onend = () => {\n      isSpeakingRef.current = false;\n      setState('idle');\n      if (wasRunning) {\n        shouldRunRef.current = true;\n        setTimeout(() => safeStart(), 300);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    utterance.onerror = () => {\n      isSpeakingRef.current = false;\n      setState('idle');\n    };\n    \n    synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\n  }, [externalSpeak]);\n\n  // Controls\n  const start = () => {\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\n    isSpeakingRef.current = false;\n    shouldRunRef.current = true;\n    setState('listening');\n    safeStart();\n  };\n\n  const stop = () => {\n    shouldRunRef.current = false;\n    if (globalRecognition && globalIsActive) {\n      try { globalRecognition.stop(); } catch {}\n    }\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\n    setState('idle');\n  };\n\n  const toggle = () => {\n    if (state === 'listening' || shouldRunRef.current) {\n      stop();\n    } else {\n      start();\n    }\n  };\n\n  const pause = () => {\n    if (globalRecognition && globalIsActive) {\n      try { globalRecognition.stop(); } catch {}\n    }\n    shouldRunRef.current = false;\n    setState('idle');\n  };\n\n  // Styles\n  const isActive = state === 'listening' || state === 'speaking';\n  const borderColor = state === 'listening' ? '#10b981' : state === 'speaking' ? '#eab308' : state === 'processing' ? '#f97316' : 'rgba(184, 134, 11, 0.4)';\n  const glowColor = state === 'listening' ? 'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.3)' : state === 'speaking' ? 'rgba(234, 179, 8, 0.3)' : 'transparent';\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{\n      background: 'rgba(0, 66, 54, 0.95)',\n      border: `2px solid ${borderColor}`,\n      borderRadius: '16px',\n      padding: '16px',\n      marginTop: '20px',\n      boxShadow: isActive ? `0 0 30px ${glowColor}` : 'none',\n      transition: 'all 0.3s'\n    }}>\n      {/* Header */}\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: '12px' }}>\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px' }}>\n          <div style={{\n            width: '10px',\n            height: '10px',\n            borderRadius: '50%',\n            background: state === 'listening' ? JSON.stringify({ text, context, user_type: 'user' })\\n      });\\n      \\n      const data = await response.json();\\n      \\n      // Handle commands\\n      onCommand?.(text);\\n      \\n      // Fill form fields if we got formData\\n      if (data?.formData?.fields) {\\n        await fillFields(data.formData.fields);\\n      }\\n      \\n      // Speak response\\n      if (data?.response?.text) {\\n        speak(data.response.text);\\n      } else {\\n        setState(shouldRunRef.current ? 'listening' : 'idle');\\n      }\\n      \\n    } catch (err) {\\n      console.error('[UnifiedBar] Process error:', err);\\n      setState(shouldRunRef.current ? 'listening' : 'idle');\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Fill fields with typewriter effect\\n  const fillFields = async (formData: Record<string, string>) => {\\n    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(formData)) {\\n      if (!value) continue;\\n      \\n      const fieldConfig = fields[key];\\n      if (!fieldConfig) continue;\\n      \\n      const element = document.querySelector(fieldConfig.selector) as HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement;\\n      if (!element) continue;\\n      \\n      setFilling(key);\\n      element.focus();\\n      element.classList.add('vv-filling');\\n      \\n      // Typewriter effect\\n      element.value = '';\\n      for (let i = 0; i <= value.length; i++) {\\n        element.value = value.substring(0, i);\\n        element.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));\\n        element.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));\\n        \\n        // Call setter if provided\\n        if (fieldConfig.setter) {\\n          fieldConfig.setter(value.substring(0, i));\\n        }\\n        \\n        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 25));\\n      }\\n      \\n      element.classList.remove('vv-filling');\\n      element.classList.add('vv-filled');\\n      setTimeout(() => element.classList.remove('vv-filled'), 1000);\\n      \\n      // Final setter call\\n      if (fieldConfig.setter) {\\n        fieldConfig.setter(value);\\n      }\\n      \\n      setFilling(null);\\n      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 200));\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Text-to-speech\\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    if (externalSpeak) {\\n      externalSpeak(text);\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    if (!synthRef.current) return;\\n    \\n    const wasRunning = shouldRunRef.current;\\n    isSpeakingRef.current = true;\\n    \\n    // Stop listening while speaking\\n    if (globalIsActive && globalRecognition) {\\n      try { globalRecognition.stop(); } catch {}\\n    }\\n    \\n    synthRef.current.cancel();\\n    setState('speaking');\\n    \\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    utterance.rate = 0.95;\\n    \\n    utterance.onend = () => {\\n      isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n      setState('idle');\\n      if (wasRunning) {\\n        shouldRunRef.current = true;\\n        setTimeout(() => safeStart(), 300);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    utterance.onerror = () => {\\n      isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n      setState('idle');\\n    };\\n    \\n    synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\\n  }, [externalSpeak]);\\n\\n  // Controls\\n  const start = () => {\\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n    isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n    shouldRunRef.current = true;\\n    setState('listening');\\n    safeStart();\\n  };\\n\\n  const stop = () => {\\n    shouldRunRef.current = false;\\n    if (globalRecognition && globalIsActive) {\\n      try { globalRecognition.stop(); } catch {}\\n    }\\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n    setState('idle');\\n  };\\n\\n  const toggle = () => {\\n    if (state === 'listening' || shouldRunRef.current) {\\n      stop();\\n    } else {\\n      start();\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const pause = () => {\\n    if (globalRecognition && globalIsActive) {\\n      try { globalRecognition.stop(); } catch {}\\n    }\\n    shouldRunRef.current = false;\\n    setState('idle');\\n  };\\n\\n  // Styles\\n  const isActive = state === 'listening' || state === 'speaking';\\n  const borderColor = state === 'listening' ? '#10b981' : state === 'speaking' ? '#eab308' : state === 'processing' ? '#f97316' : 'rgba(184, 134, 11, 0.4)';\\n  const glowColor = state === 'listening' ? 'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.3)' : state === 'speaking' ? 'rgba(234, 179, 8, 0.3)' : 'transparent';\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{\\n      background: 'rgba(0, 66, 54, 0.95)',\\n      border: `2px solid ${borderColor}`,\\n      borderRadius: '16px',\\n      padding: '16px',\\n      marginTop: '20px',\\n      boxShadow: isActive ? `0 0 30px ${glowColor}` : 'none',\\n      transition: 'all 0.3s'\\n    }}>\\n      {/* Header */}\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: '12px' }}>\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px' }}>\\n          <div style={{\\n            width: '10px',\\n            height: '10px',\\n            borderRadius: '50%',\\n            background: state === 'listening' ? '#10b981' : state === 'speaking' ? '#eab308' : state === 'processing' ? '#f97316' : '#64748b',\\n            animation: isActive ? 'pulse 1s infinite' : 'none'\\n          }} />\\n          <span style={{ fontSize: '14px' }}>\\n            {state === 'listening' && '\\ud83c\\udfa4 LISTENING'}\\n            {state === 'speaking' && '\\ud83d\\udd0a SPEAKING'}\\n            {state === 'processing' && '\\u26a1 PROCESSING'}\\n            {state === 'idle' && '\\ud83c\\udf99\\ufe0f READY'}\\n          </span>\\n          <span listening */}\\n      {state === 'listening' && (\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: '3px', height: '30px', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: '12px' }}>\\n          {[...Array(20)].map((_, i) => (\\n            <div\\n              key={i}\\n              style={{\\n                width: '3px',\\n                background: 'linear-gradient(to top, #10b981, />\\n          ))}\\n        </div>\\n      )}\\n\\n      {/* Filling indicator */}\\n      {filling && (\\n        <div style={{\\n          background: 'rgba(6, 182, 212, 0.2)',\\n    borderRadius: '12px',\\n        padding: '14px',\\n        marginBottom: '14px',\\n        minHeight: '60px'\\n      }}>\\n        {interimText && (\\n          <p style={{ color: '#94a3b8',
